## Text Elements
Q. What is the Frame Buffer size with 12 bits per pixel For 640 x 480 resolution? ^EsdyFJs5

Q. Suppose a RGB raster system is to be designed using an 8- inch by 10-inch screen with a resolution of 100 pixels per inch in each direction. If we want to store 6 bits per pixel in the frame buffer, how much storage (in bytes) do we need for the frame buffer? ^rS9C0DA0

Q. WhyRefresh Rates Matter ? ^1eWNEsEv
